add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #Removing temporary ideas
	id = annex.0
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		remove_ideas = NoDoubleAnnexItalyEvent
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Flanders-Wallonia
	id = annex.1
	title = annex.1.t
	desc = annex.1.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.1.a
		add_political_power = 60
		if = {
			limit = { has_war_with = BEL }
			annex_country = {
				target = BEL
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_war_with = WLL }
			annex_country = {
				target = WLL
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_war_with = FLN }
			annex_country = {
				target = FLN
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Swiss liberation
	id = annex.2
	title = annex.2.t
	desc = annex.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}

		SWI = {
			add_state_core = 760
		}

		every_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			SWI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = FRA
					tag = NFA
					tag = FRP
					tag = OCC
					owns_state = 16
					owns_state = 21
				}
				owns_state = 943
			}
			SWI = {
				transfer_state = 943
			}
		}

		SWI = {
			clr_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
			clr_country_flag = SWI_enemies_on_all_sides
			clr_country_flag = SWI_GER_alliance
			clr_country_flag = SWI_AUS_alliance

			set_cosmetic_tag = SWI
		}

		puppet = SWI

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			SWI = {
				set_country_flag = SWI_GER_alliance
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
			}
			SWI = {
				set_country_flag = SWI_AUS_alliance
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = FRA
			}
			SWI = {
				set_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #Take Romandie
		name = annex.2.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}

		trigger = {
			tag = FRA
			owns_state = 760
		}

		every_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					state = 760
				}
			}

			SWI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		SWI = {
			clr_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
			clr_country_flag = SWI_enemies_on_all_sides
			clr_country_flag = SWI_GER_alliance
			clr_country_flag = SWI_AUS_alliance

			set_cosmetic_tag = SWI
		}

		puppet = SWI

		SWI = {
			set_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
		}

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = SWITZ_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Bulgaria
	id = annex.3
	title = annex.3.t
	desc = annex.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
			}
			add_state_claim = 841
			add_state_claim = 106
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GRE
			}
			add_state_core = 731
			add_state_claim = 769
			add_state_claim = 184
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ROM
			}
			add_state_claim = 77
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RRM
			}
			add_state_claim = 77
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BUL
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			BUL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = BUL

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = BUL_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

					add_state_core = 76
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 80
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 80
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 875
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 875
				}
			}

			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = ROM
						is_core_of = RRM
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				RRM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
				add_core_of = RRM
			}
			puppet = RRM

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {

					}

			}

		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BUL
			}

	}

	option = { #Take Bessarabia
		name = annex.6.b

			factor = 60
		}

			}

		}

country_event = { #Serbian liberation
	id = annex.8
	title = annex.8.t
	desc = annex.8.d

	trigger = {
		NOT = { is_joke_nation = yes }
		NOT = {
			tag = SER
		}
		owns_state = 107
		SER = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				controls_state = 104
				controls_state = 109
				NOT = {
					tag = HUN
					tag = AUS
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_cosmetic_tag = AHE
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SER_CONQ
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SER_CONQ
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 4
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 841
				NOT = { 841 = { is_core_of = SER } }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						owns_state = 48
						841 = { is_core_of = BUL }
					}
				}
			}
			SER = { add_state_core = 841 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 106
				NOT = { 106 = { is_core_of = SER } }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						owns_state = 48
						106 = { is_core_of = BUL }
					}
				}
			}
			SER = { add_state_core = 106 }
		}


		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SER
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			SER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = SER

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SER_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #HUN liberation
	id = annex.12
	title = annex.12.t
	desc = annex.12.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate greater
		name = annex.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 4
					AUS = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				remove_state_core = 784
			}
		}

		# Commented out the blocks of code invovled with transfering this state to Serbia
		# Results in a detached Serbian province cut off by Illyria/Crotia under normal circumstances
#		if = {
#			limit = {
#				OR = {
#					tag = SER
#					SER = {
#						is_subject_of = ROOT
#					}
#				}
#			}
#			HUN = {
#				remove_state_core = 45
#			}
#		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = HUN
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = HUN

#		if = {
#			limit = {
#				owns_state = 45
#				SER = {
#					is_subject_of = ROOT
#				}
#			}
#			SER = { transfer_state = 45 }
#		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 784
				AUS = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			AUS = { transfer_state = 784 }
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			HUN = {
				remove_ideas = HUN_financial_ties_broken
				remove_ideas = HUN_financial_ties
				remove_ideas = AUS_part_of_the_Empire
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}

	option = { #national hungary
		name = annex.12.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 94
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = AUS
			}
		}
		HUN = {
			remove_state_core = 70
			remove_state_core = 71
			remove_state_core = 875
			remove_state_core = 82
			remove_state_core = 83
			remove_state_core = 76
			remove_state_core = 84
			remove_state_core = 789
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 91
					GAL = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				remove_state_core = 73
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 4
					AUS = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				remove_state_core = 784
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = SER
					SER = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				remove_state_core = 45
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = liberated_national_hungary
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = HUN

		add_war_support = -0.05

country_event = { #The Annexation of Flanders-Wallonia 2
	id = annex.31
	title = annex.31.t
	desc = annex.31.d
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		owns_state = 6
		owns_state = 34
		controls_state = 6
		controls_state = 34
		NOT = { is_joke_nation = yes }
		BEL = {
			exists = no
		}
		FLN = {
			exists = no
		}
		WLL = {
			exists = no
		}
		OR = {
			controls_state = 51
			any_country = {
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
				controls_state = 51
			}
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = GER
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					GER = { controls_state = 741 }
				}
				has_war_with = GER
			}
			NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 4
	}

	option = { #release belgium
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}
		name = annex.31.a

		set_country_flag = FRA_liberated_belgium
		set_country_flag = FRA_dealt_belgium

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BEL
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			BEL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		BEL = { add_state_core = 741 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				controls_state = 741
			}
			BEL = {
				transfer_state = 741
			}
		}
		BEL = {
			country_event = {
				id = annex.160
			}
		}
		puppet = BEL
		add_political_power = 20

	}

	option = { #divide
		trigger = {
			FLN = {
				exists = no
			}
			WLL = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		name = annex.31.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}

		set_country_flag = FRA_liberated_belgium
		set_country_flag = FRA_dealt_belgium

		annex_country = {
			target = BEL
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		FLN = {
			add_state_core = 6
		}
		WLL = {
			add_state_core = 34
			add_state_core = 741
		}
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = FLN
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			FLN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WLL
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			WLL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { controls_state = 741 }
			WLL = {
				transfer_state = 741
			}
		}
		puppet = FLN
		puppet = WLL
		add_political_power = -20
	}

	option = { #annex wll
		trigger = {
			FLN = {
				exists = no
			}
			WLL = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		name = annex.31.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		set_country_flag = FRA_annexed_belgium
		set_country_flag = FRA_dealt_belgium
		annex_country = {
			target = BEL
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		FLN = {
			add_state_core = 6
		}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = FLN
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			FLN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = FLN

		add_state_claim = 34
		add_state_claim = 741
		add_political_power = -60
	}

	option = { #HOL annex
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = HOL
		}
		set_country_flag = FRA_annexed_belgium
		set_country_flag = FRA_dealt_belgium
		name = annex.31.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = BEL
		}
		HOL = {
			transfer_state = 6
		}

		add_state_claim = 34
		add_state_claim = 741
		add_political_power = -60
		HOL = {
			country_event = {
				id = annex.32
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #HOL liberate
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = HOL
		}
		name = annex.31.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		set_country_flag = FRA_liberated_belgium
		set_country_flag = FRA_dealt_belgium
		annex_country = {
			target = BEL
		}
		HOL = {
			transfer_state = 6
		}

		hidden_effect = {
		WLL = {
			add_state_core = 34
			add_state_core = 741
		}
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WLL
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			WLL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { controls_state = 741 }
			WLL = {
				transfer_state = 741
			}
		}

		puppet = WLL
		add_political_power = 20
		HOL = {
			country_event = {
				id = annex.32
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy it all
		name = annex.31.g
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		set_country_flag = FRA_annexed_belgium
		set_country_flag = FRA_dealt_belgium
		add_state_claim = 34
		add_state_claim = 741
		add_state_claim = 6
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_war_support = -0.03
	}
}

			}
		}
		LUX = {

		}

		add_political_power = 20

		ai_chance = {

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = FRA_liberated_belgium
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = INT_LUX
		add_political_power = -20
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_war_support = -0.02
		add_state_claim = 8

	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of the Southern Italy
	id = annex.43
	title = annex.43.t
	desc = annex.43.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate socialist italy
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = syndicalist
				has_government = totalist
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = SRI
				is_in_faction_with = ITA
				ITA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				is_in_faction_with = SRD
				SRD = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		name = annex.43.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}

		hidden_effect = {
		SRI = {
			add_state_core = 115
			add_state_core = 156
			add_state_core = 1006
			add_state_core = 837
			add_state_core = 117
			add_state_core = 742
			add_state_core = 1002
			add_state_core = 114
			add_state_core = 2
			add_state_core = 764
			add_state_core = 1005
			add_state_core = 157
			add_state_core = 162
			add_state_core = 161
			add_state_core = 1004
			add_state_core = 838
			add_state_core = 158
			add_state_core = 1003
			add_state_core = 159
			add_state_core = 160
			add_state_core = 759
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
			}
			SRI = {
				remove_state_core = 783
				remove_state_core = 39
				remove_state_core = 795
				remove_state_core = 736
			}
		}
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SRI
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			SRI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}
		puppet = SRI
	}

	option = { #liberate republican italy
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = totalist
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = SRI
					OR = {
						has_government = syndicalist
						has_government = totalist
						has_government = radical_socialist
					}
					SRI = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = ITA
				is_in_faction_with = SRI
				SRI = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				is_in_faction_with = SRD
				SRD = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		name = annex.43.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		ITA = {
			add_state_core = 115
			add_state_core = 156
			add_state_core = 1006
			add_state_core = 837
			add_state_core = 117
			add_state_core = 742
			add_state_core = 1002
			add_state_core = 114
			add_state_core = 2
			add_state_core = 764
			add_state_core = 1005
			add_state_core = 157
			add_state_core = 162
			add_state_core = 161
			add_state_core = 1004
			add_state_core = 838
			add_state_core = 158
			add_state_core = 1003
			add_state_core = 159
			add_state_core = 160
			add_state_core = 759
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
			}
			ITA = {
				remove_state_core = 783
				remove_state_core = 39
				remove_state_core = 795
				remove_state_core = 736
			}
		}
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ITA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}
		puppet = ITA
	}

	option = { #liberate two sicilies
		trigger = {

			NOT = {
				has_government = syndicalist
				has_government = totalist
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
			NOT = { country_exists = SIC }
		}
		name = annex.43.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SIC
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			SIC = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}
		puppet = SIC
	}

	option = { #return to ITA
		trigger = {

			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = ITA
				ITA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}

			ITA = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		name = annex.43.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
			}
			ITA = {
				remove_state_core = 783
				remove_state_core = 39
				remove_state_core = 795
				remove_state_core = 736
			}
		}
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					state = 115
					state = 156
					state = 1006
					state = 837
					state = 117
					state = 742
					state = 1002
					state = 114
					state = 2
					state = 764
					state = 1005
					state = 157
					state = 162
					state = 161
					state = 1004
					state = 838
					state = 158
					state = 1003
					state = 159
					state = 160
					state = 759
					is_core_of = ITA
				}
			}

			ITA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #return to SRI
		trigger = {

			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = SRI
				SRI = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				has_government = totalist
				has_government = syndicalist
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}

			SRI = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		name = annex.43.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		if = {

		YUN = {
			exists = no
		}

			exists = no
		}

		OR = {
			owns_state = 325
			owns_state = 603
			owns_state = 601
			owns_state = 605
			owns_state = 788
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = QIE
			has_war_with = CHI
			has_war_with = SQI
			has_war_with = TIB
			has_war_with = AOG
			has_country_flag = YUN_COL
			tag = QIE
			tag = CHI
			tag = SQI
			tag = TIB
			tag = AOG
			tag = NPA
			controls_state = 608
			controls_state = 716
		}
	}

		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = YUN_COL
		}
	}

		days = 4
	}

				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT

			}

			days = 360
		}

					exists = yes
					controls_state = 17
				}
			}

country_event = { #Fate of France - CAR

	id = annex.102
	title = annex.102.t
	desc = annex.102.d

	trigger = {
		controls_state = 16
		NOT = { is_joke_nation = yes }
		tag = CAR
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = BRI
			has_war_with = NRM
			has_war_with = OCC
			has_war_with = GER
			is_in_faction_with = NFA
			is_subject_of = NFA
			has_country_flag = FRA_CONQ
		}
		OR = {
			FRA = {
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
			FRA = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = FRA
				}
				owns_state = 16
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			FRP = {
				exists = yes
			}
			has_country_flag = FRA_CONQ
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = FRA_CONQ
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 4
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			country_exists = FRA
		}
	}

	option = { #deal with NFA

		trigger = {

			NFA = {
				exists = yes
			}

			NFA = {
				is_subject = no
			}

			NOT = {
				has_war_with = NFA
				has_country_flag = offered_nfa
			}

			NFA = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = RUS
				}
			}

		}

		name = annex.102.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = FRA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = FRA
					NOT = {
						is_controlled_by = FRA
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						controls_state = PREV
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FRA
			}
		}

		NFA = {
			country_event = {
				id = annex.103
				days = 1
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = offered_nfa

	}

	option = { #FRP

		trigger = {

			FRP = {
				exists = no
			}

		}

		name = annex.102.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = FRA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = FRA
					NOT = {
						is_controlled_by = FRA
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						controls_state = PREV
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FRA
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			FRP = {
				add_state_core = 14
				add_state_core = 23
				add_state_core = 19
				add_state_core = 30
				add_state_core = 15
				add_state_core = 31
				add_state_core = 25
				add_state_core = 33
				add_state_core = 26
				add_state_core = 22
				add_state_core = 21
				add_state_core = 763
				add_state_core = 32
				add_state_core = 817
				add_state_core = 20
				add_state_core = 27
				add_state_core = 17
				add_state_core = 785
				add_state_core = 18
				add_state_core = 16
				add_state_core = 24
				add_state_core = 983
				add_state_core = 980
				add_state_core = 984
				add_state_core = 735
				add_state_core = 762
				add_state_core = 1

				if = {
					limit = {
						29 = {
							AND = {
								is_owned_by = ROOT
								NOT = {
									is_core_of = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_state_core = 29
				}
				if = {

							AND = {
								is_owned_by = ROOT
								NOT = {

								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_state_core = 943
				}

				is_core_of = FRP
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			FRP = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = FRP

	}

	option = { #Occitania

		trigger = {

			OCC = {
				exists = no
			}

			OR = {
				controls_state = 21
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = CAR
						is_subject_of = CAR
					}
					controls_state = 21
				}
			}

		}

		name = annex.102.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}

		if = {

				country_exists = FRA
			}

					is_owned_by = FRA
					NOT = {

					}

					limit = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						controls_state = PREV
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FRA
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			FRP = {
				add_state_core = 14
				add_state_core = 23

				add_state_core = 26
				add_state_core = 22
				add_state_core = 21
				add_state_core = 763
				add_state_core = 32
				add_state_core = 817
				add_state_core = 20
				add_state_core = 27
				add_state_core = 17
				add_state_core = 785
				add_state_core = 18
				add_state_core = 16
				add_state_core = 24
				add_state_core = 983
				add_state_core = 980
				add_state_core = 984
				add_state_core = 735
				add_state_core = 762
				add_state_core = 1

				if = {
					limit = {
						29 = {
							AND = {
								is_owned_by = ROOT
								NOT = {

								}
							}
						}
					}

				}

								}
							}
						}
					}

				}

		}

			}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Siam

	id = annex.118
	title = annex.118.t
	desc = annex.118.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet - Mahidol
		name = annex.118.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = GEX
				tag = RUS
				tag = UKR
			}
		}

		### Khmer Krom
		# Saigon - 286 (VIE > CAM > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = VIE
					tag = CAM
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 287 # Annam
					owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
					owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
				}
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 286 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIE = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 286 }
			VIE = { transfer_state = 286 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 286 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 286 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 286 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 286 }
		}
		# Mekong Delta - 856 (VIE > CAM > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = VIE
					tag = CAM
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 287 # Annam
					owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
					owns_state = 286 # Saigon
				}
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIE = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
			VIE = { transfer_state = 856 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 856 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 856 }
		}

		### Cambodia

				remove_state_core = 655

				remove_state_core = 537
			}
		}

				is_core_of = JAP

					is_core_of = KOR

					is_core_of = ROOT

		}

			remove_state_core = 536

			remove_state_core = 526
			remove_state_core = 645
			remove_state_core = 648
		}

				is_core_of = JAP

					is_core_of = KOR

				is_owned_by = ROOT

			}

				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = JAP

		add_political_power = -20

	}

	option = { #Okinawa

			factor = 35
		}

		}

			}
		}

			limit = {

		NOT = { is_joke_nation = yes }
		NOT = {
			tag = RWA
			tag = MAF
			tag = GEX
			tag = TNZ
			has_country_flag = RWA_CONQ
			controls_state = 546
		}
		owns_state = 869
		RWA = {
			exists = no
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = totalist
			NOT = {
				tag = POR
				tag = GER
				tag = NFA
				tag = GBR
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = RWA_CONQ
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 4
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.199.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		RWA = { add_state_core = 869 }

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = RWA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			RWA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = RWA

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = RWA_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

	id = annex.210
	title = annex.210.t
	desc = annex.210.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.210.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LBR
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			LBR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = LBR

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					LBR = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = LBR_AUTHDEM
					}
				}
				LBR = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Deutscher Liberian Bund"
						name = "DLB"
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #liberate authdem (anybody but Germany and Mittelafrika)
		name = annex.210.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LBR
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			LBR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = LBR

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				LBR = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = LBR_AUTHDEM
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Authoritarian Dem."
						name = "Authoritarian Dem."
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = LBR_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #Sardinia is asked if it wants to return to the mainland
	id = annex.232
	title = annex.232.t
	desc = annex.232.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.232.a #To Turin!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = annex.233 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
			}
			CAN = { country_event = { id = annex.235 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = NFA
			}
			NFA = { country_event = { id = annex.235 } }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
			remove_from_faction = SRD
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.232.b #No, we won't sell ourselves to a foreign power
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = annex.234 } }
	}
}

country_event = { # Sinai

	id = annex.237
	title = annex.237.t
	desc = annex.237.d

	trigger = {
		NOT = { is_joke_nation = yes }
		NOT = {
			tag = SAU
			tag = JBS
			tag = IKH
			tag = OTT
			tag = YEM
			tag = JOR
			tag = EGY
			tag = PAL
		}
		owns_state = 453
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SIN_CONQ
			owns_state = 446
			has_war_with = EGY
			owns_state = 454
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SIN_CONQ
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.237.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		add_political_power = -20
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_war_support = -0.02
		set_country_flag = SIN_CONQ

	}

	option = { # transfer

		name = annex.237.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					PAL = { owns_state = 455 }
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = PAL
						PAL = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					SYR = { owns_state = 455 }
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = SYR
						SYR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					JOR = { owns_state = 455 }
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = JOR
						JOR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				455 = {
					is_owned_by = PAL
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					state = 453
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				PAL = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				455 = {
					is_owned_by = SYR
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					state = 453
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				SYR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				455 = {
					is_owned_by = JOR
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					state = 453
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				JOR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # transfer

		name = annex.237.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = EGY
				EGY = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		EGY = {
			transfer_state = 453
			add_state_core = 453
		}
	}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Iraq

	id = annex.239
	title = annex.239.t
	desc = annex.239.d

	trigger = {
		NOT = { is_joke_nation = yes }
		NOT = {
			tag = OTT
			tag = EGY
			tag = SAU
			tag = JBS
			tag = KUR
			tag = SYR
			tag = JOR
			tag = PER
			has_country_flag = IRAQ_CONQ
		}
		owns_state = 291
		NOT = {
			owns_state = 554
			controls_state = 554
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = IRAQ_CONQ
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	option = { #United Arab tag

		name = annex.239.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = JOR
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 554
				}
			}
		}

		every_state = {

			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 454
					state = 455
					state = 554
					state = 553
					state = 677
					state = 812
					state = 680
					state = 291
					state = 819
					state = 676
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			JOR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
				set_country_flag = united_mashriq_nijato_was_here
			}

		}

		puppet = JOR
	}

	option = { #KUR/JOR

		name = annex.239.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = JOR }
		}

		every_state = {

			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 291
					state = 812
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			JOR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = JOR

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = KUR
					KUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = KUR
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = KUR
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				KUR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			puppet = KUR

			else = {
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = KUR
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
					KUR = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #only KUR if JOR exists

		name = annex.239.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = JOR
			JOR = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}

					is_in_faction_with = KUR

				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = KUR
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 291
						state = 812
						is_core_of = KUR
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				KUR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			puppet = KUR

			else = {
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 291
						state = 812
						is_core_of = KUR
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
					KUR = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to JOR ally

		name = annex.239.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = JOR
			JOR = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				has_country_flag = united_mashriq_nijato_was_here
			}
		}

		every_state = {

			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 454
					state = 455
					state = 554
					state = 553
					state = 677
					state = 812
					state = 680
					state = 291
					state = 819
					state = 676
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}

			JOR = {

				add_state_core = PREV
			}

		}
	}

		name = annex.239.f

			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = IRAQ_CONQ

		add_stability = -0.06
		add_war_support = -0.06
